//      https://github.com/GPUOpen-LibrariesAndSDKs/RadeonProRender-Baikal/blob/master/Baikal/Kernels/CL/sampling.cl
// (0, t_max], return t_max otherwise. 
// -------------------- MACRO -------------------------- 
// --------------------- ATOMIC OPERTIONS ------------------------ 
// --------------------- CONSTANTS ------------------------ 
// --------------------- HELPERS ------------------------ 
// --------------------- NORMALIZATION ------------------------ 
// --------------------- REDUCTION ------------------------ 
// --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Apple OCL compiler has this by default,  
// Assign Morton codes to each of positions 
// Axis aligned bounding box 
// BVH node 
// Calculate bool radix mask 
// Calculates a 30-bit Morton code for the 
// Calculates longest common prefix length of bit representations 
// Choose offset based on radix mask value  
// Constants
// CoordinateSpace
// Copyright 2017 Valve Corporation. All rights reserved. Subject to the following license:
// Directivity
// Do not change the order 
// Energy Field Gather Kernel
// Expands a 10-bit integer into 30 bits 
// Find span occupied by internal node with index idx 
// Find split idx within the span 
// Given a point in triangle plane, calculate its barycentrics 
// IIR Filtering
// Image Gather Kernel
// Intersect ray against a triangle and return intersection interval value if it is in 
// Intersect rays vs bbox and return intersection span.  
// Intersection criteria is ret.x <= ret.y 
// Intersection definition 
// Make a union of two bboxes 
// Material
// Multitype macros to handle parallel primitives 
// NOTE: Custom directivity callbacks are not supported at this time.
// Perform group split using 2-bits pass 
// Propagate bounds up to the root 
// Radeon Rays Helpers
// Random Sampling
// Ray Generation Kernels
// Ray definition 
// Reconstruction Kernels
// Set parent-child relationship 
// Shading + Shadow/Bounced Ray Generation Kernels
// Shortcut for delta evaluation 
// Sphere Occlusion Kernel
// Split kernel launcher 
// The bin is determined by (in_array[tid] >> bitshift) & 0xF 
// The following code is from the Radeon Rays / Baikal GitHub repository. It can be found at:
// The following two functions are from 
// The kernel computes 16 bins histogram of the 256 input elements. 
// These are already defined in Apple OCL runtime 
// This must exactly match the hit data structure (struct Intersection) used by Radeon Rays.
// This must exactly match the ray data structure (struct ray) used by Radeon Rays.
// add neutral elements 
// by inserting 2 zeros after each bit.

// https://valvesoftware.github.io/steam-audio/license.html
// if  representations are equal we consider sucessive indices 
// max neutral elements 
// min neutral elements 
// so embrace with #ifdef in the future 
// todo: linear reconstruction?

/// Specific function for radix-sort needs
